I found the issue! Look at line 266-267:```python\n@register.filter(is_safe=True)\n@stringfilter\ndef stringformat(value, arg):```The `@register.filter(is_safe=True)` decorator marks the stringformat filter as safe! This means that the output of the stringformat filter is marked as safe and will NOT be escaped by the Django template engine.So the flow is:\n1. Django template encounters `{{ value|stringformat:'s' }}`\n2. The value is passed to the stringformat filter\n3. The stringformat filter returns a string marked as safe (because is_safe=True)\n4. Here's what was done:\n\n### Root Cause\nThe issue was in the Django template files for rendering widget attributes. The `stringformat:'s'` filter was marked with `is_safe=True`, which prevented Django's auto-escaping mechanism from properly escaping attribute values containing special characters like quotes and ampersands.\n\n### Changes Made\n\n1. **Fixed `/workspace/django/forms/templates/django/forms/widgets/attrs.html`**\n   -
